3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (2 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="form-control" id="search-input-1" maxlength="128" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input has no label

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Add a <label> element with for attribute pointing to input id
2.1.1 Tastatur (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive textarea has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state

Interactive textarea has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (2 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="form-control" id="search-input-1" maxlength="128" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input has no label

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Add a <label> element with for attribute pointing to input id

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (2 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="form-control" id="search-input-1" maxlength="128" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input has no label

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Add a <label> element with for attribute pointing to input id
2.1.1 Tastatur (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive textarea has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (2 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="form-control" id="search-input-1" maxlength="128" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text"/>

Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input has no label

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Add a <label> element with for attribute pointing to input id

1.3.1 Informasjon og relasjoner (4 avvik)
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

First heading is h2, should start with h1

<h2 class="tjenester__main-title"> Helse og mestring </h2>
Start your heading structure with h1
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Heading level skipped: h1 to h3

<h3 class="events-list-item-heading text-decoration--underline text-decoration--hover--child--none"> Fagkveld om naturrestaurering i Nannestad
Don't skip heading levels. Use h2 instead of h3
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Multiple nav elements exist but this one has no label

<nav style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between;"> <div class="logo" style="padding-bottom: 20px; padding-top: 20px;"> <a href="/" title="Gå til forsiden"> <img alt="Nannestad kommune logo"
Add aria-label to distinguish between navigation regions (e.g., 'Main navigation', 'Footer navigation')
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

List contains non-li elements: ['div']

<ul class="list-inline main-links-2"> <li class="main-menu-item settings-links"> <a href="https://www.altinn.no/Pages/ExternalAuthentication/Redirect.aspx?returnUrl=https://www.nannestad.kommune.no/mi
List elements (ul, ol) should only contain li children

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (2 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="form-control" id="search-input-1" maxlength="128" name="q" placeholder="Søk" type="text"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input has no label

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Add a <label> element with for attribute pointing to input id
2.1.1 Tastatur (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive textarea has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<textarea aria-hidden="true" style='min-height: 0px !important; max-height: none !important; height: 0px !important; visibility: hidden !important; overflow: hidden !important; position: absolute !imp
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state
